 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * chrome mobile for android
 * distinct from stock Android browser
 * crmo/ is optional, only in older user-agents
 * https://developers.google.com/chrome/mobile/docs/user-agent
 * feature list
 * https://developers.google.com/chrome/mobile/
 * http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google_Chrome_for_Android
 * 
 * only available for android 4 and later
 *
 * Chrome Release Dates
 * http://googlechromereleases.blogspot.com/
 * 
 * versions after version 25 parallel chrome
 * adds additional HTML5 features to android
 * NO FLASH, WebGL (even though <canvas> is GPU-accelerated)
 * 
 * versions before 18.0 use "crmo" in their user-agent string
 * GPU-accelerated canvas, including CSS 3D Transforms, CSS animations, SVG, WebSocket (including binary messages),
 * Dedicated Workers; it has overflow scroll support, strong HTML5 video support, and new capabilities such as IndexedDB,
 * WebWorkers, Application Cache and the File APIs, date and time pickers, parts of the Media Capture API
 * Also supports mobile oriented features such as Device Orientation and Geolocation
 * -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 * 
 * "Anna" contains new browser

 * MeeGo - capacitive touch screen smartphones, running MeeGo 1.2 Harmattan operating system.
 * 
 * SymbianOS/9.3 - non-touch smartphones with larger screens, S60, 3nd edition
 *
 * SymbianOS/9.4 - touch screen smartphones with resistive touch screens, S60, 5th edition
 *
 * Series40 - Nokia proprietary OS, mobile phones with a small screen
 * S40OviBrowser - Nokia Browser for Series 40
 *
 * Symbian/3 - These are touch screen smartphones with resistive touch screens.
